O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	Oh, most noble sons, I have completed this book which is the aftermath of the science of medicine, and have filled it with its contents, and have made the end by its explanations and by its declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And it came to me in a vision that I should complete it with this treatise, which is part of the work of hands, that is to say "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work of hands is fortified in our region and is held together by all things, it has perished along with the science and decayed, and nothing remains but the small descriptions in books of the ancients that the hands have moved.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And from this comes the error and the vanity, and the minds are closed and the knowledge is distant.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation;	It seems to me that I can revive it together with the order of this treatment according to the way of exposure and declaration and abbreviation.
et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	And I will bring together the forms of cauterizing irons and other tools of the work with the explanation and preparation of it, as it is necessary.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And because of this reason that no good masters of hands are found in our time, the art of medicine is prolonged.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	And it is necessary for one who undertakes this to master the science of anatomy, as Galen says, until he knows the judgment of the limbs, and their forms and conjunctions and separations of all, and has knowledge of the bones and nerves and muscles and the number of joints, and the movement and veins moving and resting, and the origin of their issue.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc;	And because, as Hippocrates says, "the nail is not much good, and with the work is little.
et meismement en l’art de main.	And even in the art of manual dexterity.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes;	We tell you in the introduction of this book that those who are not acquainted with the things mentioned above, if they attempt to do it, may make a mistake and harm people.
ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	so that I have often wanted many times more of those who engage in this science and if they abandon themselves to science and experiment.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col;	For I saw a foolish person who lanced an abscess of scrofula from the breast of a woman, and lanced the arteries of the breast;
por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	so that so much blood issued out that the woman died in her hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans;	And I saw another foolish person who removed a stone from an old man's eye, and the stone was large;
si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	so that he took with it a piece of the bladder, and died the next three days.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	I had already been called for the extraction, and saw the position of the misalignment and the size of the stone, and if it was cut well, it would die.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie;	And another miracle that took place in our care, the Duke of our land who had his leg broken, and with the broken piece he had a wound.
et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine;	and the miracle-worker kept the broken piece above the wound, keeping it steady with great care, and did not let the wound be left open, and thus he brought it to an end.
et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie;	and he ordered that it not be displaced.
et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	and thus it remained until the leg was completely healed and the foot and came back to life.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe;	I was called to come to him, and he urged me to come to dislocate the leg;
et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	And when I felt it dislocated, it was in a place and did not feel any pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner;	But all ways of the corruption were already confirmed or the member, and it could not be healed.
et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	And the corruption did not cease to move through the member until the member was completely lost.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And I saw another method that would crush the abscess and become infected, and then inflame due to the evil of its lord.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For a pustule, when it is free of melancholic humor, does not require that one touch it with iron if it is not in a limb where one can remove everything that is corrupted.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions:	Therefore, very dear son, I advise you to know that the work of hands is divided into two divisions:
c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions;	that is to say, where it has been performed in many positions;
et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	and I will show in each part of this book where there is fear and danger.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos.	For it is better that you keep this to yourself, so that the foolish do not speak ill of you.
Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez;	If you take up your weapons firmly and steadily, and use the best method, then by God's grace you will come to safety and be healed.
et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit;	and leave behind contagious diseases of poor health;
et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	and take up your weapons from the one that makes you doubt, and be in peace so that you may come from this world to the other of glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens:	Galen says in some of his admonitions:
«Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	Do not take on sick patients unless you are called a foolish doctor.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	I have divided this treatment into three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez;	The first chapters are about fire cautery and medical cautery for the sick, and the chapters are ordered from the head to the feet.
et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	and the forms of instruments, and the irons of cautery, and of everything that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses;	The second chapters are about cutting and piercing, and of wounds and incisions, and of arrow extraction, and similar things.
et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	and the chapters are ordered and the forms of instruments.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses;	The third chapter is about restoring dislocations and twists, and similar things;
et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	and is ordered by the head of the bed, and the forms of instruments.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	As we remember from the work, it is necessary that I describe the quality of each assistant and their harmful or helpful nature.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus;	I say that the qualities of aid, and the lack thereof, are the longest speech and most subtle science and the secrets kept.
et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu;	and many wise men spoke of this, and agreed to it;
et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	and I do not speak much about it, because I keep the length.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions:	I say that fire cauterization helps universally in all matters where there is matter, whether the matter is:
c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	This is to know hot humid nature without matter, and dry nature without matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide;	In hot and dry nature together with matter, they devised none and said that the fire cauterization is great help;
et li autre dirent le contraire:	and the other said the opposite:
que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	that cauterization does not help disease that comes from heat and dryness.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour;	For the nature of fire is so hot, and should not be cured by heat from disease by heat, nor dryness;
et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	and those who said the opposite that cauterization does great help to hot and dry disease that comes in the bodies of men.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	When you compare the body of the man and his moisture to the composition of fire, you stir the body flat.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I agree with this word.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have never found it once by experiment.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens;	And in all cases, do not interfere except for those who have experienced it and know the chapter on cautery from long use, and the diversity of human constitutions, and their dispositions and causes of illnesses, and the symptoms and the space of time.
des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	We have no fear of other constitutions, even in cold and moist diseases.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And all the hairs gathered together and aligned with the cauterization.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	And know, children, that fire cauterization is a secret of healing and greater good than cauterizing medicine.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	For the fire is simple, and it only comes to the member that is cooked, and does not harm other members unless named.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation;	The heating medicines come from one member to another by removing them, and bring diseases of relief to the sick member.
et par aventure ocit lou malaide.	And perhaps it may cause harm.
Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	The fever does not hurt for its heat and for the goodness of its substance, if there is no excess.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses;	And I have found this through experience and by the length of service and study that I have put into the art, and it has been above the truth of things.
et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant;	And because I excuse the length of the word, for I do not like to give you the secret that is hidden or fire, and the quality of the work, how it breaks diseases of the body, as the philosopher says in demonstrating.
or le recevez en vos pensees.	or receive it in your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	And know, son, that they should be done at what time the cautery is to be applied, and then they should be prayed for.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere;	And I say that cauterization is suitable in all times, because the harms coming from it are removed by the help of cauterization.
et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	And even when it is cauterized, it is for necessary pain, rather than waiting for the tension that could cause greater harm to the limb.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire;	Do not think like a foolish child, as they do.
car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue;	for the disease that is healed by cauterization has no recurrence.
et il le dient ensi;	and he says so.
mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	But he is not as they think, because cauterization is only a medicine that moves the complexion, and dries the humors that cause pain, and it is more effective than other medicine for its swiftness of value, and for the virtue of its work and its authority.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut;	And it is possible that the disease comes at any time according to the humor of the patient and the part of the disease and its nature.
et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie;	And they are assembled in him the excesses by the acquisition of meats and similar things, unless if you administer cauteries to the part where there is excess and moisture, as cauteries for dense pain, and similar things, and the pain does not return.
mais ce avient poc.	But this happens rarely.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir;	And many people do not understand why cauteries are called the back of medicine, and this is so.
mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	but they do not believe that cauterization works after medicine, but rather misunderstandings, and it is cauterization of the rear of medicine because when we administer methods of healing in any disease and they do not work, then we administer the cautery, and it is better.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	Therefore, it is clear that cauteries are the last resort of medicine, not according to the intention of those who misunderstand.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance;	The ancients said that gold cautery instruments are more beneficial than iron, and they did not say what else except for the quality of gold and its high substance.
et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes;	and they said that the wounds of cauterization do not make putrefaction, but it is not to see because I have experienced it, and I have found that it is to see in some people.
et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	And gold cautery is better than iron, as they say.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez;	And whenever you heat a gold instrument, do not touch it when it is hot due to the color of gold, and let it cool first.
et s’on le chaufe trop;	And if it is heated too much;
si font au feu;	then they do at the fire.
et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	and then there is enough prevention.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	For this reason we use the fire cautery that we have already prepared for our work.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Or you have ordered this chapter about the shoulder joint from the foot, because it is lighter to find.
dou cautere olivaire	oil cauter
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	This cauterization is good for moisture and cold on the head, and it is done for two reasons: because of a disease called "soda", and because of many humors that descend from the joint to the eyes, and to the ears, and due to many dreams and tooth pain, and throat pain, and even for all diseases that come from cold, such as paralysis, soda, apoplexy, and similar diseases.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir;	The form of this cautery is that the hairs should be removed by soluble medicine changing the chief III or IV, according to the virtues and age and custom of the hair, which it can bear.
et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	Then, repeat the process of the bad joint.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis;	And then make it sit crossed between your hands, and put its hands on top of its feet;
aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz;	After, place the root of your palm above the root of its nose between its two eyes;
et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	And let your fingers come to me, if it bleeds from the wound then heat the cauterizing agent called "olivare", of which this is the shape:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant;	And put it on the limb at the sign of ink, and make by descending and stretching your hand little by little in returning;
puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit;	Then lift your hand gently, and reward the limb if you see the small bone of the shoulder;
et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit;	and if you do not see it, restart the cauterization until you see the bone as I have told you.
aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors;	then take a little piece of silk, and place it softly inside, and put it on the limb, and let it stay for three hours.
aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre;	then place a soft cloth on top.
et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	and let it stay until the burn is healed.
aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat the wound with the ointment called "tetrafarmaçon" until it is healed.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge;	And the ancients said that the longer the wound remains open, the more it purges.
et por ce si aide mues.	and for this reason, use this method.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And none of these said that one should cool the cauterization so much that a part of the bone is burned, and then one should remove what is burned from the bone, and it should be healed.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors;	And the other method is to apply the cauterizing iron as lightly as possible, and push it in as far as you can lower the bone as wide as a vermilion that women put in their hair because the humors are pushed out by moisture.
et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte;	and one should leave the wound open for a long time.
aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	Afterwards, one should cure and bandage it.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor;	And these two methods of cauterizing do not seem to be good for everyone, except in some men where there is a view of fear.
et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier;	And it seems to me that I should leave it.
car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres;	because the joints are weakened by continuous natural solutions, as we testify in other members;
et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	and even when the joint with the injury is weak by nature, and the first appearance of cauterization is more suitable and gentle for me, and from this use I work accordingly in an appropriate manner for healing.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	of the ancient pain of the main
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres;	When in general the joint comes with chronic pain that lasts a long time, one should use herbs and pills called "cochie", and cleansing of the head and eyes and plasters.
et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	and if one does the cauterization that we have already mentioned, and it does not help.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit;	Take a warm cloth for the patient who is suffering from a severe illness, and that it not too hot.
adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	Then apply the fire cauterization as we have mentioned above.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»;	After applying the cauterization on each of the horn-like protrusions of the bone, as we have mentioned before, and apply the cauterization called "vasserelz".
et est I leus en coi on met ventouses;	And place them in the places where suction cups are used.
et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os:	And raise your hand so that you do not press too hard on the bone:
li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors;	The hairs feel much greater pain in this cauterization than in others, and I will speak about that later.
et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	and it is necessary that the cauterizers of the horns be more skilled than those who cauterize the median part of the head, and this is the form:
dou cautere dou chief	for the fire cauterization
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie:	When in one part of the head sudden pain comes, and the disease is spread to the eye, and the patient is purged by medicines that are not changed, and the other cures that I have mentioned in the division of diseases have been done, and yet nothing helps:
adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	then the cauterizers do it in two ways, that is to say by medicine and by fire.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir;	The cauterizers by medicine are such that you grasp a hot iron, and remove the scab and place it on the eye of the patient, and then make the temple in such a way that you can replace the iron outside the skin;
et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres;	And when it is reset, if the bone and the joint are well aligned and left like this for twelve hours;
et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III;	then the dislocation is released and treated with the decoction of garlic, and leave the wound like this for two or three days;
puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	then apply a poultice soaked in butter until the pain subsides.
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	After the treatment with ointment, as long as they are healed;

Et est apelez «clos» por ceu que li chief est fait a la forme d’un clo ou il ait I poc de corbeure, et em mileu a une petite apparance;	And it is called "closed" because the head is made in the shape of a cloak or has a small hook at one end, and in the middle has a small appearance;
et le met sor le leu dolorous, et tien ta main et trestorne le feir un poc legierement, tant que li moitiez de l’espés dou keur soit arse;	And place it on the painful joint, and hold your hand and gently press the bone slightly, until half of the broken bone is back in place.
et lieve ta main que li artere n’arde, que est defuers, et decorre habundance de sanc.	And relieve your hand so that the artery does not burn, which is below, and there is an abundance of blood flowing.

de emigraine	of the wound
Quant tu cures emigraine si com nos avons devant dit en divisions des maladies, et ne profite mie, et vois que li cauteres devant dis de la medicine et dou fer ne li soffit mie, adonques covient il que tu eschaufes le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare» tant qu’il soit blans;	When you treat emigration headaches as we have mentioned in the divisions of diseases, and it does not improve, and you see that the cauteries before mentioned do not suffice with the medicine and the heat does not relieve it somewhat, then it is necessary to remove the cautery called "cultellare" until it is white.

de la cure de fistule par cautere	of the treatment of fistulas by cauterization
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere.	When you treat fistulas as we have described in the division of diseases, and your treatments do not work, then it is necessary for you to cauterize them in this way.

et teigne li menistres son chief entre tes mains en teil maniere qu’il ne se mueve, ne ne demoinne son chief;	and wash the instruments on his head between your hands in such a way that it does not move, nor remove his head;

aprés chaufe le cautere qui est teilz:	After heating the cauterizing tool.
et est chevez au chief si com li forme d’une penne de vouteul, ensamble la queil soit li cautere;	And secure it at the tip of the tongue, as if it were a pen of lead, and the cauterizing tool.
se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente;	If you see, it is pointed from one tip to the other, and if you see, it is also like a tent.
mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	But in any case, this that is secured is better for your work.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche;	After pressing the fistula if it is open, and in taking the pus, and drying it.
et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe;	And if it is closed, if you open it, and take out the foreign bodies.
aprés met sus le cautere chaut forment, et tien ta main au cautere a la partie dou neif ensus de l’oil, que ta mains ne faice folie;	After putting the cautery on the skin well, and holding your hand on the cautery at the part above the bone, so that your hand does not make a mistake.
et met le cautere en la graisse de l’oil, et la corromp.	And put the cautery in the fat of the oil, and corrupt it.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	If you come to the beginning of the cautery just to the bone, it would be good.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors;	If not, if you must restart the cautery again, and if you have skill, let it stay for three days.
aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers;	Afterwards, put on a cotton pad in butter, and the ointment of the desiccating wound until it is healed, and if 40 days pass and it is not healed, then put on corrosive medicine until the bone is exposed.
et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	and the king according to what he would come into his chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And there is a method of cauterizing a fistula that none of the ancients said.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu;	To fistula, and fix the limb.
aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	After putting in the fisture, insert the subtle probe of this shape:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc;	and they make with the quantity of one finger's breadth;
et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil;	and hold the hand or probe firmly, and the hairs do not move, that the plugs do not stick to their oil.
et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe:	and it is appropriate to put on top of the oil, soft cotton wool in abundance or less.
li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	the plug if the limb of the fistula, and the healthy by miraculous healing.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	And if the sinus is healed by the cauterization that we have said, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	If not, then you must administer a puncture to the nose, and return the sinus to the nasal cavity according to what is proper for that limb.
des crevaices en levres	of fissures in the lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	Many times there are fissures in the lips that are called "hair", and simultaneously in the lips of children.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these fissures as we have said in divisions, and the treatment does not help, then heat a small cauterizing iron according to this form:
Et le met hastanment en celles crevaices tant qu’il viegne jusc’a font;	And put him in those cracks until he comes just short of the font.
aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	After curing the limb of cautery until it is healed.
de l’aposteme de la goule	of the abscess in the throat
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule;	When an abscess comes at the root of the tongue or in the eye, or in the palate, or at the roots of the teeth, after it is pierced and drained and swells and becomes a fistula.
et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie:	And you treat it as we have said in divisions, and it does not improve.
adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule;	Therefore, it is necessary that you use cauterization according to the quantity of the fistula.
aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu;	After boiling or puncturing the fistula, and hold your hand until the hot iron comes to the end of the limb.
et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And do thus once or twice, after the care that we have said in cures, until they are healed.
et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin;	And if they are cured thus, it is good.
et se ceu non, si covient descovrir le leu et oster l’os corrumput, selonc ceu que vos le troverez en son chapistre.	And if not, then you must discover the limb and remove the rotten bone, according to what you find in its chapter.
dou movement des dens	movements of the teeth
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain;	When the teeth are softened by moisture and the dens move, and you treat them with medicines but it does not work, then put the head of the bad tooth in your healthy one.
aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent;	After heating the cautery with which its form will come out later in some manner, put a cane on the tooth.
et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent;	and place the fire cautery deeply, and hold your hand steady so the hairs feel the heat coming to their root.
aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit;	then remove your hand and restart the fire cautery as you wish;
aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	then fill the hairs with salt and let them soak for an hour and then rinse.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	And in a similar manner, the tooth that was moving is stabilized, and the gum softened, held back, and the moisture corrupted dried.
de la dolor des dens	of the pain of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres:	When pain from the tooth comes from cold, or there is cold or wind, and medical treatments do not help, then it is necessary to use fire cautery in two ways:
et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	and fire cautery with butter and fire cautery with fire.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain;	Fire cauterization is such that you hold butter with a spoonful of fat or water.
aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez;	Then take cotton and wrap it around the tip of a needle, dip it in the melted butter, and place it on the painful tooth firmly and hold until it is cooled.
et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	And then do it often enough until its effect reaches the root of the tooth, and if you see that dipping wool and cotton in melted butter does not help, then place a hot iron on the aching tooth and hold until the pain goes away.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide;	Fire cauterization is such that you hold a red-hot iron or needle, and it should be large enough that the heat does not reach the mouth of the patient.
aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez;	After heating the cautery, from which the form will come later, and place it on the tooth and hold your hand until the cauterizer is cooled.
fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	Do this often, for the pain will be as great on that very day or the next.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer;	And it is necessary that the hairs fill their mouth with good butter in the urgency of this cauterizer, and then wipe it off.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And this is the form of the cauterizer:
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir;	And make the cauterizer as you wish, and according to what you have.
et c’est li forme de la caine:	And this is the form of the needle:
des scrophules	of scrofula
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie;	When the scrofula is of a mucous and cold nature, and is not obedient to digestion by medicines, then heat the hair cauterization with which comes after, and have two openings for the fumes to escape to the other side of the cauterization;
et met le cautere chaut sus l’apostume une fois, ou II se mestier est, tant qu’il viegne au font de l’apostume;	and place the cauterization on top of the abscess once, or as often as necessary, until it reaches the bottom of the abscess;
et se li apostume est petis si met cautere selonc la quantiteit de l’apostume, et le laisse ensi III jors;	and if the abscess is small, place cauterization according to the quantity of the abscess, and leave it for three days;
et met sus coton moilliet em burre tant que li arsure soit ostee;	and place on top of it a soft cloth dipped in butter until the burn is healed.
aprés cure le leu d’oignemens et de tentes tant qu’il soit sanez.	After healing from burns and wounds, the limb is to be treated until it is healthy.
Li forme de la cainne:	The form of the skull:
Quant les moistors vainquent sus les chenals dou pormon, et meismement quant ce vient de froide complexion, adonc covient que li malaides soit voidiez premiers par medicines solutives;	When moisture overflows the channels of the body, and especially when it comes from a cold constitution, then it is necessary that the pains be relieved first by soluble medicines.
aprés li fai cautere a la racine de la gorge, et te garde que tu ne venir mie jusc’a la gorge, et n’ardre dou keur mais c’un poc.	After the cauterization at the root of the throat, and be careful not to bring the heat too close to the throat, and do not burn too much but just a little.

et cure le leu si com nos avons devant dit tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat the limb as we have previously mentioned until it is healed.
de la toust	of the tooth
Quant tous et maladie de pormon sont de moistors froides, et li malaides nen ait fievre ne sechor, et est li maladie anciaine, se li fai .II cauteres sus la forcele en leus vuis;	When all and the disease of pormon are from cold moisture, and the pains have no fever or inflammation, and the disease is ancient, then apply two cautery burns on the forehead in their sight.

de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
Aprés soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos et sus son costeit;	Afterwards, prick the hairs on their back and on their ribs.
aprés lieve le keur qui est dedens le titillite as dois de ta main senestre;	Afterwards, hold the curved part of the bone with your right hand.
et se li jointure est desaluee dedens, si eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners douqueil ci est li forme:	and if the joint is misaligned inside, then heat the cautery that has two prongs at the end, in the shape of:
et cauterize lou keur tant qu’il le perce jusc’a costeit, et venrait li fugure dou cautere ensamble IIII cauteres;	and cauterize the bone until it pierces through the ribs, and then bring four burners together.
et por ceu est faite cautere avec le cautere qui a III ners, por coi li figure de cauterization sunt sis cauteres;	because the cautery is made with the cautery that has three prongs, because the shape of cauterization is these four burners.
et sont li nerf selonc la subtiliteit d’une tente et c’est li forme dou cautere qui a III ners:	and are the nerves according to the subtlety of a tent and it is the form of the fire cautery that has three needles:
Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce I nerf por coi il i a VIII cauteres.	And never are they placed on this one nerve because it has eight burning irons.
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil;	After putting the cautery on, place the needles perpendicularly and hold them with silk;
aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	After letting the patient rest, do not move the limbs for a long time until it is well comforted.
Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	And if it is dislocated above, this thing happens rarely, then make fire above the thick edge of the cauterizer, or many of the cauterizers in pinching.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	For the joint is closed, and it is bound with moisture and is free from pain.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When cold and much moisture come into the stomach until it is at its condition, and they multiply the diarrhea in him, and are usual methods of cures and he does not improve, then it is necessary that the pain be soothed above his back, and he extends his legs and his hands.
De ceu en aprés li fai III cauteres I desoz la cuillier dou pis per la quantiteit d’un doi, a tout le cautere clavile, et II cauteres defuers les II costez tant que li figure des cauteres soit a III angles, et ait teil espaice entre l’une et l’autre qu’elles ne soient jointes ensamble quant elles giteront porriture;	After this, make three cauteries with the spoon, one at the worst place for the quantity of a drop, and all the cautery with the claviere, and two cauteries before the two ribs until the figure of the cautery is at three angles, and has equal space between them so they are not joined together as they go through;
et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	and let the burning instruments be such that they do not burn more than the two parts of the face, and let the shape of the cauterizing instruments be according to this form without jerking:
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme;	and if you see cauterizing with a large burning instrument in the stomach according to this form;
et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche;	and the one who has fear of this burning instrument, cauterize by pricking and holding steady above the stomach, but not according to the quantity that you see in the chest.
puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	then cauterize with the entire burning instrument called "point".
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the care of the cure that we have had before, as long as they are healthy.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez;	When the liver has pain from heat and moisture and excessive swelling, as long as it is forced out of its natural condition by excesses;
et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne li profite mie, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son haitereil;	and the pains are treated as we have said in the divisions, and it does not help them much, so it is necessary that the pains be removed from their base.
et signe d’enche III cauteres selonc ceste forme et ceste figure et ceste quantiteit sus lou foie, defuer les ypocondres, lai ou li coutes de l’ome vient;	and the sign of three cautery according to this form and this figure and this quantity on the liver, under the hypochondres, where the neck of the ox comes.
et ait d’espaice entre chaicun cautere la groissece d’un doi;	and there should be space between each cautery the thickness of a finger.
et soient li cautere dou lonc dou cors, et ne presser mie mout ta main a tot le cautere;	and let the cautery be long as the body, and do not press much with your hand on the whole cautery.
et soit arse tant soulement li moitiez dou keur, et soit li malaides drois sus ses piez;	and let it be red as much only as half of the cure, and let the pains be straight up on its feet.
et s’il ne peut, si soit gisans, et estende ses jambes, et lieve ses brais;	and if he cannot, then lie down and stretch out his legs, and relieve his arms.
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors;	And if you wish, then cauterize these wounds with a surgical tool, if you are skilled and wise in the art, and be careful not to burn too much of the body, for you would make it drier all over.
et qu’il ne viegne jusc’a boueil, car li keurs est mout subtilz lai endroit, et lou saiches por voir.	and that it does not come to boiling, for the wounds are very delicate there, and the salves to see.

s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort;	If he is in a cart, he does not feel much pain from the misalignment.
et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	And if he is on a bed, he feels great pain.

et puis seigne d’enche le leu ou li apostumes est, et puis chaufe le cautere qui est semblans au rais, de coi ci est li forme:	and then bend the limb where the abscess is, and then heat the cauterizing iron which is shaped like a thistle, of which this is the form:
Et cauterize I cautere tant que li keurs soit ars, et viegne jusc’a syphac, tant que li porreture soit toute fuers;	And cauterize with the iron until the curing is complete, and it comes just short of touching the skin, until the pain is completely gone;
aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez;	After the treatment according to the treatment of bandages until they are healed;
et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	and it should only be used by those who have long studied in the art of medicine, and by whose hands these diseases have never been corrupted.
Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	Therefore, it can be boldly overcome, and in all ways, it seems to me that it is worth leaving it alone.
dou cautere de pleuresin	The fire cautery of the chest
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere:	The ancients said that one should do the following with fire cautery of aristolochia roots:
pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois;	Take a long aristolochia root, the longest you can find, and let it dry, and let it be as thick and long as your finger;
et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe;	and grind it in oil, and take it to the fire, and cauterize the fire cautery between the eyebrow and the eye, and II small cauteries a little bit below where the hair is not;
et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc;	and two cautery needles between the fifth rib and the sixth, in declining backward a little.
et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules;	and one cautery needle at the lowest point, and the other above the stomach, and one between the two shoulders, and two on the ribs just in front of the cautery between the shoulders.
et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	and do not press your hand, but open it as if smelling something.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme;	And they said that no man used fire cautery like the razor, and they sharpened it and put it between the ribs until it came to the abscess.
et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and it jumped out of the pain, as we have said in the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work, there is fear or the pain kills now, or a fistula comes which cannot be healed.
de la mice	of the mouse
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the disease of the mouse as we have said in the divisions of treatments, and it does not improve, then they resort to three methods of cauterization that are good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	When one method is such that you make three cauteries, or four, lining up according to the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the liver cauterization that we have mentioned before;

et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and lift the chest that is in the place of the mouse, or where the hairs of the pain come from the left, and let the elevations that you lift the chest according to its curve, according to the length of the body, and the cauterization be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After boiling the two needles until the threads are perceived from the other side, then draw out the cauterizing iron, and thus you will have four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you see that it is all cauterized with three needles.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After treatment when the patient has gotten pus by long tension, and it is worthwhile to do the other treatments mentioned before.
de ydropisie	For hydropy, instruct the patient to let the h
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not useful for hydrops, except in the manner called "ascites".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat it according to the methods that we have mentioned in divisions, and your treatment does not help, then it is necessary that you make four cauterizations around the wound, and one above the stomach, and one above the liver, and one above the kidneys, and one behind the back above the spine, and one at the worst place.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cauterizations be close to the surface of the skin.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After leaving the cauterizer overnight for healing, do not let the care of the wound after the cauterization be neglected.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	And healing will proceed swiftly, and both intentions will be achieved with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The shape of the cauterizer for the belly is shown in the drawing that we have before us.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	And this one for the back is oval-shaped, as it is shown above.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the inflammation of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen to the one who is hydropathic, and they are plain of awake citron, it is necessary that you cauterize above the back between the auricular and the annular.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	Lightly touch the skin with the cauterizing tool, moving towards the wound.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, thus avoiding the yellowish part, and let the cauteries be done according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After performing two cautery treatments on each leg at the tip of the sharp needle;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	Either the cautery is long, one from behind and the other from in front, within the leg;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cautery above for a longer time to heal, which is in its place.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After the other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When the solution of the stomach comes from cold and moisture, as long as the retentive and digestive powers that are in the stomach and in the intestines are blocked, and cannot be treated by other means of treatment.
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient suffering greatly and of great virtue, then make a large cauterization across the stomach according to what he has spoken before about the cauterization of the stomach, in the cauterization circles.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and IV cauterizations around the belly subtly at all the cauterization clavile subtle, and II cauterizations above the buttocks.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moisture abundant and the pain suffering, then perform the fire cautery above the knuckle, and I cautery above each rib, and two small cauteries below the stomach, for the cure is profitable when it has good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of worms
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the tumors are at their base or one or more, and are old and are large humors cold and moist corrupted, and are treated as we have said in divisions, and it does not improve, then make cauterizations.
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	Above the spine of the back, which is all before unprotected a little and a little in triangular, and with the fire cauterization outside the belly two doses.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	And if you think that his stomach is cooled, and the meat does not cook, and one sees the face swells, then the face is given a great cauterization above the stomach, as it is previously said, and the other above the liver, and the other above the lungs with all the cauterization.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	And let the cauterization remain long.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, the limb as long as it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the cartilage that is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut the skin, if it is burned like a razor, and then put it all burned above the skin that was cut.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and let your hand move towards the base of the wound as the cautery approaches, to prevent it from burning.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	Do this once or twice, and if there is much althelul, then cauterize each one as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the healing of the wounds, as long as they are healthy.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a large cautery above the alchatim, it will have greater help.
de plaie mal curee	of a badly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the wound cannot be treated by a surgeon or opened, as we will tell you in its place, then comes a disease that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When any comes fistula, and it is alerted and given purgatives and corrupted moisture, then you must provide for the whole of a thin tent, and guard that you cleanse the tent as much as it has of preparation.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After the cautery seems sharp like a razor, and the probe is inserted into the fistula according to the amount that enters, and then restart the cautery until the corrupted tissue is removed, once, or twice, or three times, depending on the amount of tissue that needs to be removed.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and guard against fire the veins that are within, and great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the fistula goes to the center of the bladder and intestine, then guard against these, and do not make any other cuts except in the place where it is needed, and think that it is not healed.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	after healing the wound as long as it is healthy, and if the wound is not clean, and the matter is removed along with the scab, then clean that the wound is completely healed.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the matter is not removed, clean that the wound is infected, and corrode the bone at the source.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	And thus, as one of those that we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain from cold and great moisture comes to rain, and does not take the form of a woman, then it is necessary that you make the fire cauterization on both sides of the rain with the clavile cauterizer that we have already mentioned.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	And if we cauterize it in the middle, it will have three cauterizations in a row, and they will be greater help.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is small and weak from cold and moisture, and the hairs retain the urine, then make the fire cauterization in the part before the bladder, where the hairs begin to grow, and on both sides, and let each cauterization be as long as a pin.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and if you have a back cauterization, or if you have a fear of it.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and the cauterizer should be shaped according to what has been mentioned before.
de la marris	of the marsh
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the wound is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their termination is late;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, it causes great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	therefore it is necessary to make three cauterizations around the wound, as we have said of the cauterization of the bladder, and two cauterizations behind the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and the cauterizer should be shaped as mentioned before.
de la hainche	of the waist
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the thick, viscous moisture descends to the buttocks of the hip, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together.
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and is found in the lower parts of the thigh, so it is necessary to cauterize the injury above the buttocks at the hip, similar to a circle, and sign before the limb around the buttock as it returns, so that the buttock is within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if the cauterization is such as those used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if this cauterization is not present, make three cauterizations of large olive oil, and let the cauterizations be similar to all the wounds;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and the healer as long as they are healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain in the loins
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes in the side of the waist, and it is from cold and moisture, and the misalignments are cured by what we have said in the division and the cure does not work, and the disease is ancient:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	then it is necessary that you purge the misalignments of large humors from foul pills or other good-like pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After he does cauterization;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the manner of cauterization is according to the second method:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	that is to say, together with burning medicines and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cauterization is done in many ways, such as:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the back of the hipbone III triangular cauterizations in this form, and it has good depth and great, and there is between each cauterization a space the size of a thumb, and let the cauterization be olive oil.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Never cauterize in the middle of the backbone, because it has four in this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see, if you cauterize with the cauterization of the circle that we have said before in the dislocation of the hipbone;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	However, make it in such a way that the circle contains the entire chest, and all the spines are straight.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in sciatica, when the pain remains in the hip, and does not reach the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes to the thigh and leg, make two cauterizations where the hairs are, and one cautery above the ankle four fingers, on the right side a little bit.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cauteries be sharp, and straighten the spine.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the hairs feel that the pain extends to two fingers or near the knee, cauterize where it feels the pain three or four times with the cauterizing iron called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if the profession is, then make more of it;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the pain is on the side of the thigh towards the groin, then cauterize with a pointed or circular cautery, and be careful in all your cauterizations that you do not leave the cautery for too long, burning nerves and large arteries, and do not cause greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who have cauterized above the ankle of the foot, and left it too long that the leg was completely bent, and the foot also, and all the bones were perforated and corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a stomach purge resulting in death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in both parts together, apply cauterization to one and the other, in this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise say in the cauterization of the loins, because of this method, make such a needle and it should be at the top as large as a naval of a digit, or somewhat less, and it should be placed between the ribs and one prick after another at a distance equal to the quantity of a new pence;
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and let there be pliers over two parts, and they should also be like pliers, and there should be one good iron tongs.
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	and let it be heated until it is completely red and smells like metal, and then put it on the board of the back of the misaligned shoulder, and turn it over to the healthy side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and the cauterization should be done once the burning iron is removed and left for three days.
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then apply a poultice of butter, and leave the wound open for a long time.
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment of ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasis says that we use this cauterization little due to its frightful appearance, and few see those who use it;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and all the time this is a good cauterization, which can bear suffering, and where it becomes effective.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cauterizing instruments of medicine are such that you make an instrument with cuts on the edge of the door, and it is either of brass or iron at one end, and in the high part it has II us, and between each quantity of the size of a finger;
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and they are open underneath and above, and they join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After placing the board on the patient's back lying on their side, and quickly placing your hand on the board of the back;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	then pour between the two circles of the hot water which is heated by the fire I pot, and let it stand for an hour with the heat, and suffer the hairs the heat and the burning of it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it truly has the same effect as fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the burning has passed, hold the instrument with your hand and lift the back gently, and let it stand for three hours, and put on butter until the black part of the scar is removed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let it lie for three days so that putrefaction may pass;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the final help after the treatment of burns until they are healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has extended to the thigh or leg, use the same tool that you used in the groin to increase it.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the method of the hot bath, and I have written about it in the treatment of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take quicklime and live chalk, as much of one as the other, and crush them together, and put them in a new earthenware pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	or if he has a small puncture except for the point of a razor that can be closed;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and put that one in the other, and well pounded, with alum and chalk and sweet oil until there are two of them above the powders that you will have well prepared in your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and let it remain in this way until the water and blood descend, then take all of it, and pour it over the salt and over the alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And if it is very watery, it should be administered in the form of drops or cauteries for other members.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	Because it does this great work like fire, and if other medicines are cauterized in the same way as this, such as terisia and myrrh and salt with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	Galen tells us of a cure where some people were cured of the pain in the back and sciatica, and the louse was much, and he said that no other cure was made, and that they were cured once when this cure was made, and he bathed as it teaches afterwards.
