et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	And if they cannot be placed in position, then place the woman on a chair, and lift her feet up high.
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	Then, remove the seat above ground, and tie it up so that the woman does not urinate during the removal.
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	And if the hands cannot enter, and the child is dead, then use the hands that were previously placed on the buttocks, remove the child, and reset it evenly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	from the child's birth above its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes out of its feet, if it is necessary to put it up high;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it little by little until it is even;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	Then take the feet and extend them little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	If it jumps towards the toes, then command it to bend, and make it spit out the condition.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	If you must, God willing.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not lie down as we have said, gently turn it little by little until it is in the natural position.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	Then it will be perfectly fine.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come out as we have experienced, say so and take muscle powder of high, and oil of sage, and melted glue, and grind everything in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and put on the natural substance of the woman inside and outside of this plaster, then make it sit in high heat until above the ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when it is softened outside, make a garland of myrrh, and put it on, and let it sit for an hour.
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then make it sit on the seat, then make it vomit and hold its mouth and nose, and lightly press its belly, for it is about to vomit now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the child's head above its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When a child comes in this form, so put the baby's hands gently and gently;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then it should be laid on its back, and the feet hang down, and it should lie on the bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and gently fold its hands, then grasp the hands on the stomach, and remove the swaddling clothes until it is dressed all over;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not cry, then take its feet and gently move them, then move the stomach upwards, then push your hands;
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and gently feed the child.
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and command the woman to hold it until the child is born.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the issue of the child who comes out widely with a hand extended
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	You must engineer to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if you cannot bring it back, then lift the woman and go;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot go, then make her lie on the bed, and bend her knees gently;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then apply the muscle relief that I have mentioned;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not improve, then make her sit on the chair, and then study how to bring back the hand.
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and if the child is according to the natural shape, and make her spit, and command her to bend until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	of the child's neck, and have his hands spread out, and his face turned towards his mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary for the patient to soak their hand in water, then slowly and gently turn it, and lightly rub it.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	And when it is even, place the natural muscle balm of aloe and oil, as we have said, then command the patient to move it slowly.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	And when you have done this, place it on the seat, and command the patient to sit down.
et la fai esternuer.	And make them spit out.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same way for all the second joints
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes to this way in the second joint, then adjust the second joint to your angle, until the moisture is drained.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	And if it cannot be adjusted to its face and neck, then adjust the back, so that it is not held back, and let the adjustment go.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	Then push the child inward, until you have placed it as it should be, and command the woman that she does not give birth again:
adonques si istra legierement.	then strain lightly.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the issue of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	it is said that children are born many times, and sometimes in giving birth, three or four:
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange thing, and it happens often.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	these are strange things, and they do not live if they are not named:
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they are multiplied, and they are divided by the midwife who gives them names, which is tied to the belly:
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and never come out as naturally as others do, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they come out harshly, as we have said the treatment should be, and if there is a subtle breeze, and do it quickly and lightly as it does.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do so as it is worthwhile for health.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Never are they formed in the first, second, third, fourth, fifth, sixth, seventh, or more than fifteen years old, and are all formed in the shape of a child by the measurement of the wise glorious, and it is fitting that the breeze should heal everything, for perhaps similar things happen to them.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	Do it according to what is appropriate.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When treating a woman for a dead or live baby, as I mentioned in the section on labor, and it does not come out, and you are forced to perform surgery with your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	if it is necessary that you remove from the woman if she is of sound health and has no accident or fear of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	if it is necessary that the woman be placed on her back, and her legs bent down, and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the midwife the tweezers of the other part, where she is tied to the bed so that she is not treated with the delivery of the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the mouth of a tumor with moist mustard seed mixed with garlic and fenugreek seeds, then insert the juice of these oils and mixtures into the tumor;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	then gently close the tumor, then check if the needles are suitable for the skin, and if the patient is not allergic, then let it drip on their forehead;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	if the needles are inserted into their eyes or in their throat or in their mouth or in their palate or behind the beard or on the forehead or beside the costal cartilages, and if they drip on their feet, then let them drop on the soles of their feet or on their chest or on their shoulders;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	And it is necessary that he dye the wound with his right hand, and place the cauterizer between the fingers of his left hand, and hold the cautery lightly in any of the ways we have mentioned, until he reaches the empty thing.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the shape of the wound:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then hold against the other wound, or if you have skill in this matter, so that the extraction is equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	Then hold it equally by moving from one side to the other, in order to move, and let the wounds be dyed with equal dye, as is the shape:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if a part remains, oil some of its bones with oil, and put them in that part, and pull the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if none remains, put this bone or more on top of the limb, and do it as much as it all goes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes in front of the other, and it cannot be brought back by tightness, then you must wrap around the injured part, until it all goes out;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	then put the bandage in the joint of the foot or at the heel, and so you must do in the other hand, and to both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child is large and tight at the outlet, or has an acute angled head, it is necessary that you push the spatula-shaped bone between your fingers, and making the head and straightening the acute angle.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you break it with the tool called "almidach", from which the shape comes with the tools or chapter that follows this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and thus make the same action if the child has a large natural head.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull the bones with pliers, and if the child jumps and is held by the forceps, it must be cut as much as possible until the blood that has been issued stops.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	If she cannot get out, then break the copper piece with which you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	And if it is inflated in the belly or under the ribs, then you must prick it until the pus flows out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	If it is above its feet, then it is light attraction, and the direction to the mouth of the marsh is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is hard in the belly or in the groin, then you must squeeze it out with a cloth wrapped around your hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	And making the belly or the groin, as much as the pus that flows out.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	And if the other member is broken, and the patient remains, then boil the bay leaf in water, and bring it to the mouth of the wound.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then apply heat or cold, and treat it accordingly;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth is swollen due to an abscess that has come, it does not need to be pierced, but rather things that are wet and heavy should be administered;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and apply plasters, and soak in hot and moistening baths.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	and if it is on the side of the chest, and you can make it even, then treat it as we have said for a living infant;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if you cannot make it even, then treat it by applying pieces and leave nothing of the second part.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, apply what we have said about abscesses that come from the marsh.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	And if blood comes out, it should be stopped with immediate pressure, and other treatments applied.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	I saw a woman in whose womb an infant had died, then consulted the other with regard to that one, and it also died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, some abscesses appeared in the groin, and they swelled so much that they burst, and then began to cause great pain.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I went to the doctor, and he thought for a long time, and could not close the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied strong adhesive, and it pulled out some bones, and after some time, others came out.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very surprised because the belly does not have bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I dressed the wound, and in the process broke bones, until the woman was no better.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And she remained long in this condition, and it was only a little improvement from the bloodletting.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I did not remember this chapter until now because when the masters find an unusual thing, they know how to provide help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	bring the marble back to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	This comes after the form of the presser, by which we have the books.
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	And at the second turn, to the second question of the two joints.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	However, the horns should be more slender than the restrictor, and should be made of smooth or box wood.
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	And its mouth should be one and a half inches wide, and the edge of the trees should be, and a span and a half long.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	And between the two joints should be two stoppers of this same wood, which are firmly fixed in one and the other, half a span long or a little more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	et these two incisions are made in the mouth of the horse when turning the two corners.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, which appears more subtle and lighter, should be made of smooth or boxwood, according to the appearance of the tongs.
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and it should have two incisions, such as you see, of one span in length and one wide.
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see that the horse's mouth is open with all the instruments, place the woman on the bed, the feet down and the legs spread, then insert the two incisions incised together into the mouth, and hold the head of the instrument between her teeth.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then work your hand with all the tools, as you have done with evenly made needles, according to the quantity that you see opening the mouth of the marsh, until the bail does what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These tools are all above, and they are multiplied in their likenesses;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when the master has them all arranged, the work is more difficult, and higher for those who have more of them.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	If you do not disregard the tool that you have not matched, for its need is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second one is retained at childhood, it is necessary that you command the pain to retain its hair, and then make it spit out the conditions, and hold your hands to the mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she jumps for the sky, well then.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take the pot, and make a poultice or covering, and put herbs that can open the mouth of the marsh, such as calamint, anise, chamomile, cassia lignea, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or any of them, should be cooked or poured over boiling water above the fire.
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	Then put a cloth or poultice from the pot in her mouth, and the other head in the mouth of the marsh, and let the steam come into the marsh.
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then make her spit it out, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the patient sneezes repeatedly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if she remains after this treatment, and is not much improved, command the bath attendant to rub her right hand with oil of sesame or mustard plaster, and then apply it to the affected area, and ask for the second one.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And when she finds it, grasp and extend it slowly and straight, so that the husband does not hinder its extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	But move it slightly to the right and left, and then pull it out.
si venra et se desaerdra.	If it comes out and disperses.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the husband's mouth is also stretched, we have said the cure of expectoration and fumigation of herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	If she is not of all that we have said, then guard that you do not follow her;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is advisable that what is at the mouth of the wound, that you tie it to the belly of the woman, then clyster with the four-ingredient ointment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	if the pains and bring back, and come force;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	but always, when she vomits if comes bad smell to the stomach and head, and bleeds the pain.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	If therefore fumigations inconvenient to that:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	none of the ancients have experienced fumigation of watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument used to fume the woman during retention of flowers and the secondine is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is similar to glass, and one puts the head subtly in its place, and the wounds are large over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and either the smoke over the coals, and the lice until they are killed, and then start another one.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the foundation pierced, but it is stupefied by some subtle poison:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	so it is necessary for the midwife to pierce that poison at its proper place, and not pierce too deeply with the sharp instrument, and cover the wound so that it does not touch it;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply a poultice of mallow on wine and oil, then the healing ointment until they are healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will not set, place or press a splint on it, and let it remain for some time, and it should be strengthened as the child wishes to go into rooms.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes comes the stink of pus from a wound or an abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	if it is necessary to cover that pus:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	if they are treated, as we have said of the dog's excrement.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula from the base
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from below the foundation are noduled, and grosser than those coming above the foundation, or in the space of two parts, if there is one fistula or more;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	and when that nodule is old, it works and increases the moisture above the white or subtle bowels, and sometimes those fistulas persist.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And they are known by the fact that there is vomiting or vapors when the pain causes vomiting, and sometimes it happens that some words come out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if there are fistulas that perforate the bladder, and perforate half of the penis.
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And they reach the joint of the ribs, and penetrate the throat.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the fistula passing through the base, and not passing through.
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	And it is that you should strike your sharp index or base, and insert a thin needle of silver or iron into the fistula when there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if he has twisting, then beat him with a thin tent peg, or the hair of a horse, until you feel the tent or the hair at your hand.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and he does not come from pustule egestion or windiness or vomiting, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	so that it does not pierce through.
si te haste dou curer.	if you are in a hurry to cure.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula is persistent near the bladder or near a urine conduit, if it allows urine to pass, and cannot be healed by medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	if it has pierced up to the joint of the thigh, then beat him with the tent coming from the body.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no twisting and the invention of the pain is around, then it is because he has been bitten by a snake, and there is no medicine or soundly by cauterization.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And in these fistulas, there is no cure except for patience and the vanity of those who try to heal them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In that one which is not ancient and not persistent, with hope of healing by iron, as I have experienced, and it is that the pain hides between your hands on its back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and the patient's legs up to his knees, and his knees bent towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then pour water or mud, if there is twisting, until you see the tent come out.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the pain is felt around the foundation, then it is necessary that you insert your second finger, feeling as if the tent has pierced it;
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	And it should be discovered or you sense between your teeth the sphacel or the char, then scrape that it is finished;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if not to grind a little that we cannot heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is said that one can heal all, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid that is made, if it is to heat the subtle cauterization according to the width of the fistula, as it is already said;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and the whole mouth is put into the fistula, until it comes out of the base;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times, until you scrape that these charred pieces are removed, which are similar to an arrowhead;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then the treatment of broken bones in butter, until that bone sets, then the treatment of cauterizing charcoal and sealing.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is thus healthy, it is well.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If so, no other method can be used;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the bone is between, and does not pierce through the foundation, and between the tooth and the tent a thick layer of charcoal or sphagnum, and you see the fistula at which the covering points.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if the covering of the beginning of the fistula, and is pushed back before the tent, and then the cauterizing after, until it reaches the top of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and he will be delivered from the tent, and fall.
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then one must believe those charcoals that seem like a goose feather, and not remain doubting.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if you cannot pull it out, and cut between you and the work, then cauterize with fire or medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery assembles two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the burning of these charcoals applied, and the draining of blood and the drawing out of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then the cure of moldy tents is to boil or crush them in a mortar, until the liquid is poured out, and the charcoal is burned in the liquid;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then cure the wound of boils soaked in hard charcoal, and the dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is healed, it is healthy and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if the fistula comes from just above the foundation, and is distant from the body, then press on the top or foundation, and ask what it is.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent, and there are two threads or sutures or charcoal, where it is about to pierce, there is no other remedy but hope and faith, by administering one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it off at the base, or if you can, you put in tents and treat it as first aid.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not move too much in the first few days, so as not to cover the foundation that holds the base, and the excretions come out through the opening.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	If fortunately it will be healed, or you remove that covering and the bandage since it is cut below the base, or by tent or by other appointed instrument.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then put your finger in that wound which is in the sore, as much as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Then study to restore the wound, and to delay the fistula in the part before the base.
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	If it is a lighter thing to the pain.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes fistulas are in this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	And when you put the tent in the fistula, and it is where it costs the base below the skin above, then take a tent perforated at the head in this form:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And you push the wire through it, and push the probe along the entire length of the wire into the fistula until it reaches the top.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is persistent in the margin of the foundation downwards, then hold the thread of that which is punctured, in such a way that you bring your own or the foundation upwards.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	And trace the head of the thread, and gather the two parts together, and hold one against the other, and let it rest for one or two days.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And keep it under no pressure until the thread covers those that are between the two, and heal.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then treat the wound until it is dried and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not perforate, then try to puncture it in all possible ways that you can, unless it is too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it does not matter to make the sutures so deep if it is too deep, and then treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spiny stone that they make the fistula is very sharp and one-sided;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other hand, not, because we do not know what we should not know, as you see here:
des emorroydes	from the worms
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	There are two kinds of dislocations:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	Or they are in the foundation, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and in this case, blood is involved, and there are one or more, and they are under the foundation and at the base of the foundation;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	But those that are underneath have little moisture, and they are cut or a little sharp or a little bloody, and they have the color of the flesh;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment of those who have them in the foundation is that you command the patient to urinate in different rooms, until the foundation is clean and the child appears;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you hurry, and it can be done with pliers, or you hold it at your fingernail, then cut it at its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if they cannot hold it by their moisture, then take them with a cloth, or a rag, or a piece of linen.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And strain them with your fingers, then cut, and powder with any hot powders that are in place of the fire cautery.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Or you cauterize them as it is said in the book of fire cautery, then treat with other treatments until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the foundation cannot come out, then cauterize the painful part with biting and rough laxative to clean what is in the foundation, so it can come out openly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	When the painful joints are pressed, and if their roots are deeply rooted, then the light treatment is applied.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And you should press them with your finger or pliers, and cover them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed, and do not fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	If it is necessary that you mend the wound in this way:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a sharp needle, and thread it onto a needle, and then pull the thread from above and make the needle pierce from the other side, and turn the two threads away from the needle, and if it is wide.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	Hold the thread firmly, then release the thread, and extract the needle, and do likewise with all others, and leave it for a time to allow the excess blood to flow.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place above the wound a piece of cloth soaked in red oil or cerate, and place it above the wound, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then let it remain until they heal, and when they are healed, apply ointment and other remedies until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	drily with the hands where the base is founded
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	often found dry where the intestines are, and due to constriction of nature, and when the disease is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	If it is necessary to reset at the tip of a small bone or with your finger, the surface of which does not allow it to become moist.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then the healer should position it as it should be.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot be positioned, then restart the scraping more forcefully than before until it is clean, and let it be scorched.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then the healer should make it clean.
dou fremit	high fever
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Mice are a small appearance deformed on the chest, and they go deep into the flesh.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and never find the cause, and it feels like a fever of coldness, and it spreads throughout the body, and more than in other parts.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the healer should take a quill of a goose pen, or a strong pen of a vulture, and place that quill on the coldness, until the circle around the coldness is complete.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand to all the soreness until you remove everything within the heat, and put it in front, and extract the heat from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, do this in the form of a rain or iron dog according to this shape, and be subtlely removed and drawn upwards:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Do not let go, to hold on to both and press.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see that the heat is cauterized, as it is in front or in the chapter of cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the shape of the splint
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Never made a salve with silver, lead, molten gold or tin;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	And never made those small and large instruments according to those that you will bring.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those who are to be nursed in the care of children and those who are weak and painful, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the bandage is small and large, depending on how wide the belly is tied in this way:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	And if there is a disadvantage where the belly is tied, as you see, and the bowel is inside, then you must pierce;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	And say to one of the costal arms, two on the right side, and one on the left.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And let the belly be filled with medicines from a pig's bladder or parchment, and perforate all around with small holes, and put one inch of space between each hole, then wind a thread tightly around in an X or around, and gather the belly as if it were a goat.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	And when the medicine is inside, tie the thread strongly to the instrument in front of a strong thread, then apply a poultice.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And this is the shape of a circle.
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and oil the head of the poultice with oil or egg yolk, or a similar thing, then apply it lightly.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	then the ministers pour water into his two hands together, until it is all clear, then remove the cloth, and lift the patient's legs to a sitting position, and if he wishes to get out of bed, then help him as much as possible.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if he sleeps all night, it is even greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you apply the poultice in the illness of diarrhea, and the medicine wants to come out, start it again as long as it is healthy.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if they are hemorrhoids at the base, or an abscess, then the cloth should be as gentle as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of a gentle cloth over the skin where it is stretched:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have said in the division, the treatment of wounds.
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We will tell you about the treatments for hands and medicines, according to the completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are different according to what they are made of, and according to the parts or wounds that are made, and from which they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are done by piercing with a spear, and cutting with a sword or dagger, or of lance or staff or arrow, or similar things.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or that are made according to the lessons of the body, such as a wound that pierces through the neck, or the head, or the foot, or the belly, or the liver, and similar members.
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment of every wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, because the memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound comes or the head is not broken, and if it is a puncture of a similar thing, and the skin is completely torn and is large, and you slightly doubt an abscess:
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	if you quickly heal the head itself if it comes soon from blood of the wound, and whether the healing is on the affected part:
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and avoid the pains of overeating of wine and heavy meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to heal, let him soften his meat, and do not drink wine, and do not change his food:
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	Put on the wound, if it is suppurating and pus comes out, moistened cotton with rose oil or sterilized wine.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no suppuration, put on the wound, if it is fresh and full of blood, and it does not move due to air, powder that I will say a little later.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound has moved, put on some bandages until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like a tailor's cut and similar, and the lips cannot come together by tenting, then stitch them together by sewing, as I will say about wounds of the belly, from sewing.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	If the wound is exposed to the bone, and can be moved, and only holds at one point, tie it.
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	Then treat the wound with medicine, and replace durable leather in its place, and command the patient to eat soft foods, such as tests and cooked grain, like chicken, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find any suppuration or pus on the skin, and it is not attached to the bone, then scrape it all away, and pour in vinegar, then heal.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein, without cutting it, and it cannot be stopped by medicines, then tie the artery, and if you find any suppuration or pus in it, dislodge it, and tie it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if it does not help, then cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere:	And if these wounds are small and simple, then the treatment is light:
et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	and you put in this powder that sours as soon as the air touches it.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est:	And the manner of the powder is as follows:
pren encens une partie;	Take a part of incense;
sanc de dragon II parties;	blood of dragon two parts;
chalz vive III parties, et le poudre subtilment, et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	live chalk three parts, and the powder finely ground, and fill the wound, and let it set firmly and join to all its blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle;	and then bind it well, and leave it without movement until it does not swell;
car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	for one should not use the medicine until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And never use chalk alone when one does not have incense or dragon's blood, but that the wound has moved.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the wound has moved, immediately in its place, do not put any other of this powder;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but place some digestible ointments, or hair of barley flour made of quicklime and honey, until it flows out.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then the healer performs other treatments until they are healthy.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if a bone fracture comes with the wound, and it is small, then extract it with delicate pins;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you afterwards about the main fractures.
de la plaie dou col	of the neck wound
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound comes from the neck and it is simple, there is no difference between this and the main fractures, but if the neck nerves or the artery is cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerves, then there is no other method than to leave the treatment and not put anything restricting, because it harms nerves and causes them to retreat;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and do not place anything sharp on the wound, for the substance of the nerves is cold, and its continuity with the brain, which is one of the highest members.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce, et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	but let the medicine be gentle, like how wounds are washed with warm water, and mixed with rose oil, and bandages are also washed with warm water, and other remedies according to this manner, and keep them moist.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then bind it with a bandage, and treat it until it is healed.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and full of pus, then prick or lower the limb.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the artery is cut and blood flows, then stop it, and bandage it, and cauterize as necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va, si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	And if it is pricked by a thorn in the neck, and cut off, or if the wound is cleaned, and the conductor is kept, by which the meat goes, if the wound is on the back of the neck, and do not touch the neck but put it back according to its natural shape.
et puis l’estraint avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then gradually tighten the bandage, and leave it for some time, then treat the wounds until they are healed.
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	And if the wound has made an impression on the bone, and it is necessary to remove it.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse, et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	And if there are pieces of bone, and you can remove them all, and those that you cannot remove, leave until the wound has healed, and then disinfect and align the wound.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	If the wound is fresh, then apply powder on top of the powder I have mentioned.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if he has bone in the wound and there is a fistula, then treat it as I have described in his chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound of spear or of dagger
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne:	If it is a spear or sword wound, and the wound is deep, look to see if there is any ventricle (air pocket) that the hairs do not reach:
saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	then shave off those hairs that are mortal:
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont, et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	if it is not deep and the wound is fresh throughout its entire length, then do not apply powder or bandage for the first hour for the blood that does not stop flowing out of the body, and let it return to the heart, and cover the pain:
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie II fois le jor;	but I apply an attractive ointment, and tie it twice a day.
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor, et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie III jors, ou IIII, ou plusors;	and if you do not have an ointment, put dry cotton in the wound to soak up the moisture, and let it rest on the wound for three days, or four, or more.
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’estraingnemens d’alainne;	if no spasm occurs, nor trembling of the heart from another cause;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see good conditions, cut open the wound to save it.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	cure the other wounds and other treatments, until they are healed.
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule;	and if it cannot heal and work, then cut open the fistula.
si la cure si com on doit.	if the care is done as it should be.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or dagger cut, and it is simple, or worse, at the back, then the care for what is in front.
s’elle est grans, de cousture;	if it is large, of stitching.
et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	and if it is small, of powder, and if it is pressed into the bone, and has broken off pieces, then remove the wound, and the traces if they are necessary.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not necessary, then let the wound rot, it will help the extraction.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and other wounds to other members are as the judgments as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	abdominal rupture
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The dislocations of the belly are large, medium, and small.
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	Of the great wound, the intestines never jump out once, or the nerves of the intestines, by which they are inserted.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans, por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	And the sewing is more painful, and never is worse than the small wound than the great one, because one must put the intestines back in, if not they are put back in from top to bottom.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes, et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres II.	Therefore, because the intestines swell quickly when they feel the cold, and they are put back in more easily, and because the medium-sized wound is worth less, because one must roll the intestines back to their place like the others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc IIII manieres:	And the tear of the belly is according to FOUR methods:
les II costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre, et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et II autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	The two common sutures in the belly wound are in the seam of the belly, and the seam of other wounds of the chest and TWO other private seams are common to other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And all in all, they are more suitable with the seam of the belly, and I will say each one and explain it.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer, et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des II manieres:	I say that when the wound is small, and nothing of the intestine is protruding, and there is no other thing to be done, it is best to put back by one of the TWO methods:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit, ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	either because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said, or because the intestine is swollen by the heat.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	When it is cold, warm it in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou I mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement, ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique, et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	Soak a sponge or some dry bread only in hot water, or boil it in hot, sour, and salty water until the intestine swells enough to be removed.
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And never do this again, as it may cause harm and should not be repeated to avoid discomfort.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites, car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	And when you see the swelling separate, moisten the intestine with hot or cold water and cook the meat, as this will make it easier to enter.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter, make a small incision in the instrument used to remove tumors.
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille, que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	and the first care is to move the wounded part, that we should not cut without great necessity.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	And these are the tools for the cutting:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	If you cut within the beak and not without, and see the shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer, si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre, se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	And when the wound is enlarged and the intestines have jumped out, if you can put them back in their natural form according to their own place, because this is good.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre, si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	When the wound is wide and in the lower part of the abdomen, it is necessary to place the injured part on its back, and raise its legs higher than its head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre, si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz, et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des II parties si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	and if it is in the lower part of the abdomen, place the head and the foot higher than the other parts, and also if the wound extends to one of the two sides, make sure that the injured part is higher than the other.
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus, you should manage as I have described in severe and moderate wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet, puis aies entre tes mains I ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main, et assemble les levres;	For small wounds, apply what you have prepared, then place your hands between the wound and the patient's hand, and administer healing ointment that covers the entire wound and closes the lips.
et c’est la maniere commune de costures, et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie, puis laisse des le chief de la plaie I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait I boin fil fort;	And this is the common method of stitching, and you should grasp one or more needles, according to the quantity of the width of the wound, then leave the tip of the wound a little space, and there insert a needle with good strong thread.
et perce les II chiés dou cuir avec les II chiés dou siphac, qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie, et assemble les II chief dou siphac les IIII ensamble;	And pierce the two needles through the two pieces of skin, which is outside the skin, until you make it pierce from that part, and gather the two ends of the thread together.
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de II pars, puis assemble les II chiés de la plaie avenanment, et puis laisse I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	Then the thread of a doubled string around the needle of one part, then gather the two ends of the wound evenly, and leave one inch of space, and insert another needle.
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille, et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles, tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	Then tie the wound with a thread as you did with the first needle, and do not stop doing this according to what you know about needles until all the wound is closed.
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses, car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	And let the needles be of medium size, between thin and thick, because thin needles cover the entire wound, and too thick ones cannot enter well.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	Therefore it is necessary that they be of medium size.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir, k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	and should not be placed too far from the edge of the skin and flesh, lest they pierce and open the wound before sewing.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir, et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir, et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and then cover the wounded with needles, so they do not poke the bad hair at night, and put bandages or cloths on the wounded with needles to keep them in place, and leave them until the wound is sewn.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies, car il i soffist une aguille ou II.	And this method of sewing with needles is more suitable for small wounds, because it requires only one or two needles.
Li seconde costure si est commune, et est que tu assemble les II chiés dou cuir et les II chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait I fort fil moien;	The second method of sewing is common, and it is that you gather the two pieces of flesh and the two pieces of skin together with one needle and a strong thread in the middle.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz IIII ensamble, si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	and when you have perceived these joints all together, if you reset the needle in the part where you began, in the manner that one does with the drills.
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and put a space between each stitch the thickness of a small needle.
ceste costure sevent li home, et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre, qui estoit navrez d’un coutel, et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant, et issoit des intestines bien II palmes de grant, et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	This stitch heals the man, and I sewed a wound that one had in the abdomen, which was made by a knife, and it was the wound more than one palm of great, and it was the intestines two palms of great, and it was the wound inside the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit XXIIII houres fuer, et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a XV jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	I brought back the intestine after it had been for 24 hours missing, and the wound was dressed with 15 hours, and cured, and was healed.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And the man had been judged that he would die, and it was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en I leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and did not care for it with bandaging, for I was in a place where none were found, nor any medicine.
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel II fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and I put moss twice a day on the wound, and washed it with honey water until it was clean.
Or vos dirai les II propres manieres de cousture:	Or I will tell you the two main methods of stitching:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and the thread from the part behind this inside.
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille, et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	When it has pierced the curved part on the right side, then the head of the needle or the thread where you have put the needle, and make it pierce from the other side of the part inside behind this.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz, et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and the understanding of this stitching is that you sew as the tailor does the fur, and you leave one side of the seam once, and bring it back from another side, until the stitching is entirely completed.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement, si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les II parties ensamble naturelment, et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	The second method of stitching, which Galen properly describes, is such that some do, who assemble the two parts naturally together, and apply one end of the seam to the other end, in a similar manner.
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement, et laisse les II chiés dou syfac;	Take a needle or one end of the arrow near, and pierce that part alone, and leave the two ends of the seam.
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, as II chiés dou syfac;	Then turn the needle, and pierce it through the part before this, from below upwards, as for the two wounds of the throat.
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en II autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Then pierce both through the part before this, from below upwards, in the two other wounds of the other shoulder.
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And this is the most common method of sewing and stitching.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent, c’on doit coudre le ventre a II aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	If anyone says this word, and no one testifies to it, then one should sew the belly with needles, where there is thread in each.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	And one should insert one needle from one side and the other from the other side, in the manner of those who sew corsets.
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre, si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	and it is more painful than other parts of the abdomen.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgment of the wound is such as the judgment of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee, si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout;	and it is that when you cut open the fresh wound to its full depth, and as soon as the doctor has moved it, you should replace the intestine and the skin.
puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char, et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	then apply the powder of incandescent charcoal, and if the doctor has moved it, then apply any ointment that is present until the wound heals.
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and sew up the wound, and be sure to clean the surface and the inside.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat the wound as with others, until it is healed.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel, et le remue II fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	And if you do not have medicines, put it on as soon as possible, when it starts to bleed, with old cloth, and move it 20 times a day until it is healed.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you have no business with other medicines in many positions where the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz, si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset, et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	And if you doubt that the wound does not communicate with the main members, then it is necessary to massage gently with oil of cold or red oil, and put it inside the angles, and remove from the joints;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient, si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	If he feels pain or nausea in the abdomen, and often occurs, then cluster him with black wine vinegar, and immediately if nausea comes to the intestines.
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And the puncture of the inside, and the salves that when it is the large intestines, it is lighter to heal than the small ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez, et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	The intestine called "jeun" cannot heal when it is exposed, and this is due to the smallness of the veins that are, and because of the subtlety of the whole body, and its proximity to the nature of nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the pus jumps from the wound, and put it back as the intestines while it is fresh.
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, car il i a voinnes et arteres;	And if it is old and becomes green or black, then you must tie the limb that is black, because there are veins and arteries.
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien, et met les II chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	then remove the thing that is between the ligaments, and put the two fingers hanging from the part of the wound away from the wound until the extraction when the bones chip, and the wound opens.
de la routure dou boueil	of the breakage of the bone
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite, si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes, por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	When the intestines are punctured, and the wound is small, if it can be returned to some people, because I saw that a man was gutted by the belly of a lance.
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac, et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and it was the wound on the right side of the stomach, and it was inflamed and became a fistula, and in it was the excretion and the ventosity.
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I put care according to what I could, and did not stop until it was healed, and the wound closed.
