la nature si revenra li brisure;	nature will return to the fracture;
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then it should be filled with cotton, and leave it in this way for some time, until it is healed.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	When the tooth of a finger or the woman's is broken, if it can be restored as we have said in the bone of the shoulder;
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	and these broken parts are not hidden from him who puts his study and practice to it, and heed my book.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	For the broken part means in many positions the right way of restoration:
enten le donques.	therefore understand it.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	In the tooth, when it is broken, take a goose quill and insert the tooth;
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	then wrap it in cloths and leave it for three days or more, and it will heal quickly.
de brisure avec plaie	of fracture with wound
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	It is necessary for one who has a fracture with a wound, even if it is large, such as the bones of the ribs or shoulder or similar, that they be cleansed immediately, so that the cleansings that we have mentioned bear witness.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the wound is clean, and if the dressing of vinegar, if you have nothing else, then begin to restore the fractured bone in the same hour, or the next day, if there are no pus.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	And if pus comes, then leave the restoration until the next day, as long as the pus is abated, and do not touch it on the following day or quarter, for you would bring about bad accidents.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	And if the broken teeth appear above the gum line, it is necessary that you gently place them in your hands, with slight extension.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	And if the extensions are not equipped with you to make it even with your hands, then bend the arm at the elbow with this iron instrument, which is of iron, and has seven or eight spans in length, and the width is according to the amount of the wound;
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	and because it is necessary for the mirror to take three or four, according to how much he has in each breakage treatment;
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	and let it be round and a little thick, that it does not pour out at the compression above the member in your work, and let it be narrow behind, and thick in the middle in front, thus:
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	And it is called "palainche", because it should be placed on the top of the head's bone.
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	and it is applied once, as long as it regrows, and they should be evenly placed one against the other.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	And if the fracture is subtle, and the splints cannot well hold the bone, then it is necessary to cut the head of the bone until the splints have hold.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	And if you cannot reset the bone, as we have said, then use an appropriate tool for this purpose, such as a saw or a chisel, to your power;
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	then file away what is remaining in the bone of roughness and small scratches.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	And when the bone is returned to its place, and the pain is great afterwards, wait until it is not in its natural place.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	If you do this until it is in its place, then wipe the area with a sterile black vinegar cloth, and properly if it was in that state;
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	and do not place anything on the wound or put anything else where there is oil, so that there will be no putrefaction and corruption.
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	then administer elixirs when you have restored the bone, and leave the wound open, and cover the covering all around, according to the size of the wound, and be careful that the wound is not compressed with the break.
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	and many times have done this to the foolish ones, and have caused the pain or death or corrosion of something every time.
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	and let the binding be softer and more gentle than other breaks.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	And if the wound is bad or large, and you doubt that no evil accident has occurred, as we have said, and you alleviate pain at the limb, then it does not matter to place leeches on it;
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	but rather wrap around, instead of leeches, hard cloths, and tie them.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	And when you see after one or two hours that the wound is bleeding again, remove what you have put on top of all the blood, and apply healing ointment, such as Tetrapharmacum and similar.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre II fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	And it is necessary that you move the limb twice a day, in the morning and in the evening, as long as it is sound and healthy.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	And it is necessary that the limbs be arranged in such a way that the bow can move lightly.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	And if they continue to protrude, and it cannot be healed but remains bent, saw off the small pieces of bone, because it is necessary that you sew the wound with a tent, and remove all those unnecessary pieces that cause pain.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	And if a fistula comes to the limb, or in any other way of corruption, then it is necessary that you heal it, according to what it says in its chapter before.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	And when the bone is broken, and open above the limb, as the bones of the ribs or shoulder, and other similar large bones, do not pull it out, for many times they die, but leave it until it can heal;
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	perhaps it will fall off after 20 or 30 days, then treat the wound, if you can.
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	and if you cannot, leave it.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	of blows that come from the welding
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	We often see after the health of the broken bone, especially near the joint, and it is a bad thing to see the shape of the limb;
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	and perhaps cannot do its natural works.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	Then take care if it is fresh:
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	if you administer astringent medicines, such as aloes, incense, and myrrh, and sarcocolla, and similar things, so that you do not use any of these things or all together, and mix them with stiptic wine or with abundant honey or with vinegar;
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	and place them on the nose out of reach, hold them firmly, and do not let go with your hands for a while.
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	then dislocate it again, and start another one until the dislocation is overcome.
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	or hold firmly on a piece of wet clay well-made;
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	because the property of clay is that it removes all swellings from the limbs.
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	and if the dislocation has already become hard like a stone, and it is necessary to remove it, then the copper above, and making the excess apparent.
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	or you cut it with any knife until it is removed, and the treatment until it is healed.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	a weak limb that is after the garrison
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When the fracture of the bone is restored, and the limb remains weak and delicate afterwards, this often occurs for many reasons:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	because one is due to the fact that it was too tightly bound, and was not loosened as it should have been;
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	or because there were too many bindings, and could not reach the necessary movements of the limb;
ou por multitude d’arosement;	or due to a multitude of swellings;
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	or because of too great movements, and not enough rest;
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	or because it has little blood in its body, so it is weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	And the treatment is that you relieve the pain, and make the body tense, until the swelling is not multiplied in it;
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	and the assistant bathes, and gives joy and ease.
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	then places poultice on the limb, so that the poultice attracts to the great swelling, and the heat often from hot iron, until the swelling is drawn out of the limb.
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	and returns to its natural shape.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	a twisted limb after healing
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the limbs are twisted after restoration, and the bones broken open, and the shape of the limb is deformed, nevertheless it does not lose its natural work.
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	if one does not believe the people who say that one should break the limb entirely, and many have done this in our land.
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	And these works are blamed, and great harm comes from them, and perhaps the death of the patient.
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	Therefore, if the dislocations and torture are severe, it is necessary to apply hot water, or mollifying herbs that are boiled, such as valerian, roots, and melilot, and similar things.
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	And the mollifying plaster is made as follows: with good adhesive, and you take valerian root and cook it with goose grease or linseed oil, and make a plaster on top.
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	Or you take dried figs and grind them with linen thread, and similar medicines that soothe the pain.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	And never is it necessary to apply continuous and prolonged pressure with wet hands on the dislocation.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	And allow movement in the limb every hour.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	And if the deformity is awake and hardened, like stone, and it needs to be removed with the knife, if it fits just above the bone, with a slight incision;
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	and put on a bandage and leave it to heal.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	Here begins the book of dislocations
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation occurs when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation comes to none, it must now be returned against the grain.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	For if it delays, the swelling increases, and perhaps if it is reset, it returns to the bone;
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	therefore, it does not fit to move it to the joint where it swells:
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	often causing pain and other injuries;
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	therefore, when it arrives, if the pain is healed, then leave it, until the abscess is calmed;
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	Then raise the limb with hot and oiled cloth, then gently reset it, and treat each member as it would be cured in its place.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	And I have ordered the chapters on the dislocations of the shoulder joint from head to foot.
des mandibules	of the mandibles
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	There are cases where the mandibles are dislocated downwards, and the dislocation of both is in two ways:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	or they are slightly out of place but softened a bit.
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	or they are completely dislocated, hanging downwards, and the tongue from the mouth cannot hold it, nor can he close his mouth, and his tongue is wrapped with speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When the dislocation is small, it often returns in many positions.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if it is completely and accomplished, then you must reset it quickly and not delay.
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	And in such a manner that the minister applies pressure to the bad joint, and places his finger slightly off one of its roots within the dislocation of the mandible within the mouth, if the dislocation is of two parts;
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	and the other hand is free, to make even.
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	And commands the patient to relax his jaws, and move them from all sides.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	And the mirror moves evenly, until it returns to its place.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if it is not possible to reset them, immediately if they are both jaws together, then apply hot and oil-soaked cloths, until they can be gently reset.
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	Do not delay in resetting, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	And when they are returned evenly, and the mouth of the misaligned joint is tightly closed to soften, then put wool cloths soaked in a thick paste made of rose oil and wax, then lightly bind it with soft bands.
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	and let the misaligned joints lie on their backs, and their shoulders be between two cushions, so that it does not move to the left or right, nor strive to move, but take light food, until the pains are removed, and the jaws are healed.
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	Then feed it lightly what it wants, and do not strive to open its mouth to eat and drink, until the jaw is well healed and healthy.
Et se les II mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if the two mandibles cannot be reset to their proper position within an hour, and they are not converted back to their original shape, then fevers and sweats become common, and possibly diarrhea, and possibly vomiting of clear fluid.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	And when you see this, then shave it off as it is deadly.
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	and often killed those who had it, in seven days.
de la forcelle	of the forceps
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The forceps cannot be removed from the side without causing further damage, and it is not reset once dislocated, and one can feel it.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	And the restoration is such that the pain lies silently on its back, and extends its arms;
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	and then press the limb firmly to your palm, and it will return.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	then put on the plaster and the bandage, and hold it in place.
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	and the patient who is behind the back cannot evacuate.
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	if not, and if it evacuates once, then reset the limb as we have said.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then place the plaster and bandage on top, hold it in place, and command the patient to rest until it is healed.
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	And immediately bring back the dislocated shoulder when it is back in its place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	of shoulder dislocation
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	It is not dislocated except by three methods:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	one of which is that it dislocates at the part of the shoulder blade to the outside.
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	and the second is at the part of the shoulder blade to the inside.
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	and occasionally dislocates at the part above, and this happens rarely.
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	and it does not dislocate behind the shoulder, and it does not dislocate inside for the nerves.
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	and often it is reset incorrectly, especially for those who have little strength, because to these it goes quickly.
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	to those who have enough strength, it goes slowly and returns slowly.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And sometimes happens to some people, a fracture or crushing, and the shoulder swells with an abscess, and they think it is dislocated by this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	Therefore, you must test it until you are certain.
et adonques encomence la cure.	Then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	And it is known that a dislocation occurs when it goes back to its place, and you will find between the sick shoulder and the healthy one a clear difference.
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	and you will find at the top of the shoulder a hollow, and outside the joint, on the top of the shoulder, as if it were an oss.
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	and cannot move its hand to its wrist, nor move from any movement.
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	and similarly, if it is dislocated above, it is not hidden, for you see it clearly at the shoulder.
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	and this manner of dislocation is only to be reset when it is new, or when the patient feels pain.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the manner is that the caregiver gently lifts the hand of the patient above, then places their fingers outside the shoulder, and resets the joint above to its place.
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	And the caregiver gently lifts the hand, and stretches it upwards, then places it outside.
si venra hastanment.	If it comes quickly.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it does not come as we have said before, then it is necessary to bathe the wound in hot vinegar;
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	and the remedy should be softening and soothing, such as a decoction of salt, fenugreek, and melilot in hot water, and it should be applied.
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	Then the wound should be placed on the patient's back, and a soft pad of even linen, not too thick or too thin, is placed under it, then the patient's foot is placed on top of the pad, and the shoulder is gently lifted, and the hand is drawn towards the wound;
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	and other ministers tie up the head of the dislocation, so it does not move down.
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	the shoulder is now completely back in place, and if you see if it stays like this:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	and that you make sure it is placed by someone who is stronger than the dislocation.
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	and that he is on the right side of the costal, and below the shoulder of the dislocation, and lift the dislocation up, so that the dislocation hangs in the arm.
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	and other ministers pull the hand of the dislocation down towards the stomach.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	And if the pain is too light, then with it nothing heavy can be done, and the dislocation returns now.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	And it is also reset in another way:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	and is of a long, thin branch in the earth, which the patient should be as like the dart, and not too thick nor too sharp.
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	then it should be placed outside the pain, but with a soft cloth underneath, and the hairs should be aligned along the length of the arrow.
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	then it should be extended by the other hand in a different way, and the joint will return to its place quickly.
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	and if it does not return for all these things that we have said, then perform this treatment:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	take a long, thick branch of about four inches wide, which has the top rounded to enter into the joint from outside the shoulder, like this form:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	then tie above the shoulder with soft cloth, which was not a remedy for the pain, then remove it from the side of the pain.
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	and extend the arm above the long one, and tie the remedy on the long one, and the arm at the top of the hand, then put the arm over the edge of a wide shield, and let the hands hang down from the other side:
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	the joint is now healed.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when she is healed in any way, it is necessary to place a bandage of equal linen over the shoulder, then apply the poultice with powder from the mill, with incense and a little oil, over the entire shoulder and around, then remove the bandage from the shoulder evenly, and return the limb to the poultice, and embrace the hand at its neck, and let your hands remain thus.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	and it is better that he move little, until the limbs are comfortable, for it will heal faster.
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	then move more after three or four days, and move it.
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	If it is stiff and cannot be softened, then it is healthy.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	And if the joint is very strong due to moisture that has come, or for other reasons, it is necessary that you administer cauteries at three points, as it is placed before or in the chapter on cauteries.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	And if you do all of this, and after seven days it dislocates again, and the joint does not hold, and cannot raise the arm above, then cut the nerves at the head of the shoulder are torn or stretched or softened.
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	and cut that the joint never returns to its place.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	The dislocation that is behind the knee and the buttocks, or behind, is made by impact, and extension of hands, and there is administered another oil.
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat until it is healthy.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And if after healing the limb swells and moves poorly, then apply the hairs many times, until that swelling is relieved, and returns to its original state.
de la dislocation dou coute	of the shoulder dislocation
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	When the shoulder joint is dislocated, it can return to its place with points, and with points it returns.
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	And it has been dislocated from all parts, and even in front and behind, and the dislocation is not yet repaired, for one can see it well and feel it.
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	And it becomes dislocated according to each shape.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you join the misaligned ear with the healthy one, see it openly.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	For the joint is cut, and cannot bend the arm, nor touch its shoulder at all.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	And it is necessary that you reset it as soon as possible, for if it comes when the joint is set, it would be painful to reset.
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	And perhaps it cannot be reset at all, especially when it is in the back.
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	It is worse than other dislocations, and causes more pain, and perhaps it kills the patient.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And the restoration is, when it is such that one can bring it back, that you extend your hand to your two hands;
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	and its arms are spread, and the hands of the master are held according to the direction of the wrist, back and forth, and press the joint at its root together, or at the base of the palm, until it returns to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is in front, it returns when he doubles his hand to his hand, and holds the root of the palm that is dislocated.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it does not return to its place, administer strong extension;
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	and that two masters extend the arm and hold it, so that it does not move during extension;
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	then turn the arm from every part, then that you have wrapped a double cloth long and wide;
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	When looking at the joint, if there is any oil to soften the joint, then apply it, and then gently move the joint until it returns.
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	And when it is in place, apply a dry poultice with some urine, and then strain it, and put the arm on the back of the painful part, and leave it for some time, then release it.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	And if the joint is firm in its place, then release the ligament, and leave it.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	And if you see that the joint does not strain well, then restart the poultice and the ligament, and leave it in this way for some time, until it is firmly put back.
puis le deslie.	then reset it.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	And if he feels stiffness after the resetting of the joint, and it moves, then bathe and rub it well, and press until it is relieved;
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	or you place a fat sheep's tallow on the joint, then leave it for a day and a night, then remove it, and let it enter or bathe in;
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	and when he feels better, rub the joint immediately, then place the tallow again, and then enter or bathe in.
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and thus do it two or three times until he is healed;
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	and if you see, then place wet mud warmed with butter on it, and press it;
si revenra a sa disposition.	it will return to its proper position.
li dislocation de la main	the dislocation of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	The joint of the hand dislocates easily, and its return is lighter than other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	However, it is necessary to return it to its place quickly, as soon as it is dislocated, provided the skin is not inflamed or there is no abscess forming.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	And the return is that you place the misaligned hand on a table, extend the injured hand, and hold it evenly so that it places its palm over the appearance of the joint, and push until it returns.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	However, you must check if it is properly aligned.
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	Then place the misaligned limb on a table for extension and reduction.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	And if the dislocation is at the back of the hand, place the patient's hand on a table, and the other person places their hand over the appearance of the joint.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	If it returns now, that's good.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	If not, apply soothing plasters and let it rest until it can begin again.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	And if it cannot be borne, and you cannot put it back in place after some time, the joint will remain twisted.
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	and not move the misaligned part until the hand is wrung dry, and cannot strain anything at all.
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	Then check if the tendon or artery is cut.
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	If there is no other method, it is to cauterize the wound with fire from the outside, and perhaps there is nothing else that can be done.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse V jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	And when the hand is in place, put the poultice that we have said above, then strain and leave it for three days, then remove and leave it thus.
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it cannot be moved well, and there is no swelling, then boil water and rub it until it is healed.
de la dislocation des dois de la main	of the dislocation of both hands
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	Never reset the fingers of the hand at any part, never to the back of the palm or to the belly;
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	then the finger remains, and push the dislocation to your pouches as long as it returns, then support the head of the finger, and bend it towards the part where it is disjointed;
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	and leave it there for two days, then put it back in place that day;
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	and bandage it as we have said, and the dislocation from the day, and the movement, and the bandage again;
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do this often, until it is tight, and just as you did before, if it is dislocated in the belly of the hand, do as you have done previously, until it is healed.
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	and do the same when it is dislocated elsewhere.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	dislocation of the spine in the back
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When the spine in the back or neck is dislocated, and there are many dislocations, there is no cure, for the patient dies from the pain.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	And the signs are such that the excretion jumps out without will, and it cannot be held, and often the limbs become soft, or the two arms or the one leg.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	And often the neck moves to the four parts.
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	That which moves to the back is called "gilbositez".
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	The cure is such that you reward those who have it from childhood:
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	if there is no cure or healing at all.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	And the one that comes from falling or from similar things, they said in ancient ways of healing with great words, or it does not help at all;
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	but I have abbreviated it according to my intention, and I have formed instruments in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	I say that in the gibosity that comes from the worst part, there is no skill or health;
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	and similarly that which comes directly in the second ribs, and one cannot heal except for that proper one which comes from the back, as I said.
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	and let the hairs be stretched out over his face in an even line, and hold the eyes open so he does not blink.
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	then apply the poultice to the forehead in a thin layer, and the other to the feet, and tie one bandage around the limbs outside of the joint, and the other around the hips, and the groin, and the knees.
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	and both caretakers tie the bandages, one around the head and the other around the feet, among the two poultices.
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	and they should be well tied, the poultice as we have said, and the blindfold places his palms over the spine, until he recovers.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	If it does not return to its place by this treatment, take a three-armed board, and lever it off, and the pain should be on the side, and push the chief of the board away from the pain, then put the middle of the board on the spine.
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	and put the injured feet on the other end of the board, and press well, until it returns to its place.
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	and if you see, do it to the thumb that turns to the hand.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	And it is that you fasten two bands at the head of the pain of an arm of great, and towards the feet two others, and between each band, outside and inside, a handspan of long rope.
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	and say in each incision, "I turn you back, and let the incisions be firmly in the earth, so they do not move.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	and between each two incisions, make one turning incision, so that the wounds may turn back, and say in the two turning incisions, "two small incisions of a palm's length, to turn the turning.
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	then bind the wound that is among the ribs to the turning towards the head, and the other wound towards the feet at the other turning, and each of the ministers turns their turning along the whole limb, and the masters put the needle evenly as we have said.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when it is even, place a drying plaster with abundant honey on top, then apply compresses, and then the tip of a tablet of three fingers in length, which will hold the bone of the spine together and the part of the spinal cord intact, then tie it with a bandage as we have said, and use the subtle pressure of binding until it is healed.
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	And if nothing comes in the end of healing, then medicines that are softening and soothing must be administered, with the remedy that we have said before.
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	And never administer a piece of lead, and if it appears in the back spine of the back, then be careful that it is not a dislocation.
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	and it is the bone that opens, for which we should not have presumption.
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	by chance it would bring death.
des dislocations de la hainche	of shoulder dislocations
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	It is known that the joints of the back and the joints of the shoulder come only in dislocations alone, and do not come like other joints;
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	and the joint of the back is dislocated into four parts:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	backwards and forwards, and front and back;
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	and more inwards than that, and less dislocated front and back.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the knowledge of its dislocation inwards is such that when one joints the bad leg with the good one, it is longer, and more open than the good ones, and cannot double the bad knee to the fire;
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	and is the joint which is inflamed from abscess, because the patient's chest is full.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of one who comes after this is that these accidents are contrary to those before.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the signs of those who have it in front, so that they can well straighten their leg according to the completion;
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	therefore, does not double the groin with pain, and if they want to make it move, it cannot go forward, and it holds its urine, and inflames the ankle, and when it goes, it passes over the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of one who has this after are that he cannot spread his groin, nor double over, and that leg is more bent than the other, and the anger is softened, and the shoulder is dislocated to the side of the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The return of this similar sign of dislocation is that you reward it with the ancient dislocation, and it stays according to its disposition, if there is no cure;
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	and there is no need for him to have presumption.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And in this case where the dislocation is fresh, and it is of four types of dislocation, if you have time to return the joint, extend and retract it, and move it to the left and right;
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	perhaps it will return, and there is no need for other treatment.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return in this way, then you must apply a strong minister, and extend the leg strongly at two hands, or at one hand that is tied above the knee;
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	and other ministers extend their hand above in a certain way that they bite their hands from their elbows, then squeeze it with a soft cloth over the knee;
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	and others tie the head of the joint;
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	and extend it up and down once, until the pain is lifted from the ground once and remains suspended.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of extension is common to four similarities, and if the dislocation has returned, as we have said, it is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If not, then you must put care to its appearance.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When the dislocation is in the shoulder, you must first put the pain on its healthy side, then place the joint above the root of the arm, and the limb that is outside the arm, then extend the joint above the arm and towards the forearm;
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	then take other assistants to hold his arms, and grasp the thick arm of the painful shoulder, and extend it behind in a proper manner:
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	if it returns to its place now;
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	and this type of dislocation is less severe than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot close it in this manner that we have said, then you must tie the two hairs of the misaligned joint together with a strong thread above the two heels, and above the two ankles, and let the misaligned leg be stretched out two fingers more than the other;
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	then it should be hung from the top of a stick, and let it hang two arms' length from the ground;
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	then command the minister to grasp the back of the neck, and let another ministers hang with the misaligned joint, who grasps the back of the neck, for the joint is now returning quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is in the shoulder, if it is pricked as we have said in the one with gout, and you hold the joint properly above the misaligned leg, and also above the foot.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	Then put two bandages, one at the top and one at the bottom, then fold the bandage between the ribs on the misaligned side.
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	And place wet cloths around it, so it does not dry out, then extend each of the healers towards him, and let the patient hold the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, it's good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, place it on the table, and press it as we have said in the gilbosite, and grind the bad parts against the clean side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is in front, it is necessary to extend the misaligned leg quickly, as I have said.
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	and place the painful part above the bad joint, then press with the other hand, and stretch it downwards towards the groin.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is in the shoulder, it does not require extending the joint downwards, nor lifting it upwards, but it should be as it was when dislocated from its place, as we have said for the position of the two shoulders;
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and it should be above its face, and the arm stretched as we have said before, and one must press on the joint at the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	and it will be fixed when the joint extends its legs, and they will be even;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	Then bend the knees, apply the ointment, and place a bandage on it, so that it does not move.
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	And rest it for three or four days, then reset it, and apply the ointment again.
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	And if you see that they are even, then reset the bandage as before, and leave it for three days.
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	Then reset it again, and make it move vigorously, until the limb is comfortable.
de la dislocation dou genoil	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The shoulder joint is dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	That is to say, from inside and outside, and behind.
et ne desalue point devant.	and do not reset before.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the signs are that you command the patient to bend his leg at his hip, and if he does not straighten it at his hip, then you must reset it.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the restoration of all is that you make the patient sit straight, and extend his leg if he can, and put your back against his face, and his foot on yours.
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	Then take his knee in your palms, and pull it towards you, then bend the two sides of the knee correctly.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	And other assistants extend his foot, until the knee returns to its place, and the signs are that he straightens his leg lightly at his hip.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	and apply the plaster on top, and make the leg stiff at the hip for three or four hours, then release it.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and do not work the injured limb until the limb is comfortable.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the member is not straight, administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the ankle dislocation
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The feet are never splinted and never fully dislocated, inside and outside.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the signs are that the knee is swollen, and test before the part where it is dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	the re-attaching is light, and one should gently extend it to their hands when it is only slightly swollen.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is dislocated quickly, then you should straighten the injury correctly, and hold it with one hand on the leg, above the knee;
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	Then hold the string with your right hand, and then with your left hand twice, then stretch it upwards, and beat the string hard against the top.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	And do this twice, as we have said, by pulling and stretching the string;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	If it comes back, it is good.
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	If not, restart the work, for it returns.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	And if it cannot return in this way, then lay the injured limb on its back on the ground, and firmly fix a splint between its thighs, and wrap bandages around it, so that it does not bend the injured limb.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	then the servants apply the poultice to the chest, and other servants stretch the cloth to his hands or to the limb, that he may tie it around the neck of the wound.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	then each servant stretches evenly, and the bandages are placed between the ribs of the wound to retain the wound as it is stretched.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	then the servants place the hands evenly on the dislocation, and other servants apply the poultice to the sound leg at the side, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it goes to the point, if the plaster and douche are applied above, and the bandage is formed, and the cloth is tied to the leg, and the nerves which are above the ankle behind, that the bindings are not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	then leave it for two days or three, and if its joints are weakened, strain them.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	then reset it on the third day or fourth, and let the pain last for four days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	and if it goes before that time, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if an abscess comes, it is necessary that you pacify it, as we have said elsewhere, until it is healed.
des dois	for two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the two are dislocated, if they should be gently extended towards labor, and this is a light matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any part of the body or limb, it is necessary that you make the pain sit above one leg plain or above the table straight, and put your hand on what opens these joints, then press your hand firmly until it returns.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	and when it is even and there is no opening, put the sole of your hand on a flat table with two fingers, then strain it firmly and leave it for three days, then reset it.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let him rest, until he is well.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wounds and of dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound comes with the dislocation, and one wants to restore it, often times it kills the patient:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	if you are not presumptuous in the cure, if you are not wise in the art and have not used it for a long time, and if you are not merciful and slow, do not be harsh:
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and at the beginning of things, use calming incisions on abscesses, and leave the wound in God's hands, if you do not see hope for health;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, then reset the limb at once, as soon as the abscesses come.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	When the member is set, administer things that reduce inflammation and heal the wound, as it should be, with dry bandages.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if the dislocation is fractured and the bones are small, decompose them, and do what we have said in simple diseases.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	And guard against entering the path of fear, as I have said, for it is better for you according to your Creator, and by the knowledge of your armor and your body.
